Letter to the Editor

To the Esteemed Editor of Shen Bao:

Greetings. Upon investigation, the news item concerning the Zhenru International Radio Communication Station, translated and published in your newspaper on the 4th of this month, as carried in a Mainland newspaper on the 3rd, is completely inconsistent with the facts. In addition to sending a letter to the Mainland newspaper for correction, we hereby issue the following statement: (1) The International Radio Communication Station being established by the Ministry of Communications has one American-style and one French-style shortwave radio transmitter each. All payments for the equipment have been made in installments. All construction matters are specifically planned and carried out by the Preparatory Office for the International Radio Communication Station, organized by the Ministry of Communications. All staff members of this office are domestic personnel appointed by the Ministry, and no foreigners are involved. (2) Both the American and French radio companies have dispatched commercial representatives and consulting engineers to Shanghai for consultation on all matters. However, they are all in an advisory capacity and have no direct authority or management rights. (3) For the convenience of international communications, the Ministry of Communications has signed service agreements with American, French, and German radio companies. The principle is that all radio telegrams from our country to European and American countries will be delivered or relayed by these companies, and all radio telegrams from European and American countries to our country will be delivered by our radio station. The sharing of telegraphic fees is separately agreed upon and mutually settled, with equal benefits as the guiding principle. The Sino-American service agreement is valid for ten years. (4) In order to seek independence in international communications, our country has purchased equipment from American and French radio companies to build its own radio stations. There is absolutely no such thing as the American company funding the construction and undertaking it for ten years, as reported by the Mainland newspaper. If it were as described, how could the Ministry of Communications propose to various submarine cable companies to cancel the existing exclusive contracts? The above four points are requested to be published in your newspaper's "Letters to the Editor" column, so that the people of the country may understand the truth and not be confused by foreign propaganda, thereby thwarting their imperialist conspiracies. We would be most fortunate.

With respectful greetings,

Preparatory Office for the International Radio Communication Station, Ministry of Communications

October 4, Year 19

Incoming Items

Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau's Animal Carcass Rendering Plant 140

Regulations for Bidding on Oil Skin, Bone Residue, and Small Intestines

(Approved and implemented by the Municipal Government on September 25, Year 19)

(1) The oil skin, bone residue, small intestines, and other items for this bid come from the animal carcass rendering plants at Xuejia浜 and Wusong. (2) The term for the winning bidder to exclusively sell oil skin, blood bone residue, intestines, and other items is one year, with the start and end dates to be determined separately. During this period, all products must be completely purchased. (3) The price for oil is calculated per hundred jin for both white oil and meat oil. The price for skin and small intestines is calculated per piece and per strand, respectively. The price for bone oil residue is calculated per hundred jin. Payment is made according to the actual quantity. (4) The highest bidder is qualified, and the second-highest bidder is the backup. (5) When receiving the bidding paper, bidders must first pay a deposit of 1,000 silver dollars to the Municipal Finance Bureau if bidding on oil, or 500 silver dollars if bidding on skin, blood, intestines, residue, bones, and other items. They must receive a receipt and wait for the opening of the bids. The deposit of unqualified bidders will be returned immediately after the opening of the bids. The deposit of the backup bidder will be returned after the qualified bidder signs the contract. (6) Bidders should fill out the bid form according to the format and submit it to the bidding box set up by this bureau within the deadline, ready for public opening on the due date. (7) The qualified bidder should provide a reputable guarantor within the deadline for filing and undertaking. Failure to do so within the deadline will result in the forfeiture of the deposit, and the backup bidder will be called in to fill the vacancy. (8) During the exclusive sales period, the bidder may not request a price reduction due to low market prices or other reasons. (9) When the rendering plant has one dan (approximately 100 catties) of stored oil, skin, blood, bone residue, or intestines, the bidder must transport it away. The maximum delay is two days, and the price must be paid with the goods without delay. Transportation costs are borne by the bidder. (10) Bidders may choose to bid on all or part of the oil, blood, skin, bone residue, intestines, and other items produced by the two plants. (11) The items bid on are only allowed for industrial use and must not be used as food privately. Violators will be severely punished. (12) If the bidder violates Articles 2, 8, 9, or 11 of these regulations, the guarantor shall be fully responsible. (13) If the items stored in the plant cannot be bid on successfully multiple times due to various reasons, the Health Bureau may select the highest price and submit it to the Municipal Government for approval to handle it through retail or auction methods.

Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau's Operational Rules for Animal Carcass Rendering Plant 141

(Approved and promulgated on September 25, Year 19)

(Article 1) These detailed rules are formulated in accordance with the provisions of Article 5 of the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau's Regulations for the Animal Carcass Rendering Plant. (Article 2) The staff of this plant may be transferred by the veterinary technicians at any time to gain experience. (Article 3) If important equipment and items of this plant must be purchased, the technician may state the reasons and report to the head of the responsible section, who will then submit it to the director of the bureau for approval before proceeding with the purchase separately. (Article 4) The accountant and administrator of this plant should fill out two copies of the daily income and expenditure items according to the specified form and submit them to the bureau, and prepare five copies of the monthly income and expenditure statement for verification, storage, and transfer. (Article 5) When the deposit reaches 100 yuan or more, it should be submitted to the bureau immediately, and then withdrawn when needed. (Article 6) For scattered expenses within ten yuan, the accountant and administrator may consult with the veterinary technician for advance payment if there is not enough time to ask for instructions, but the details must be explained in the income and expenditure report for verification. (Article 7) For all dead pigs, cattle, and sheep, regardless of size, the owner will be subsidized with one silver dollar per pig or sheep and ten silver dollars per head of cattle, but no subsidy will be given if they are smuggled and sold, and discovered. (Article 8) Whoever reports the smuggling of dead pigs, cattle, and sheep, and it is discovered, will be awarded two yuan, which should be the subsidy given to the owner. However, the staff of the plant must not claim this bonus. (Article 9) No subsidy will be given for dead pigs, cattle, and sheep that have been dissected and sent to the plant for rendering. (Article 10) Whoever transports dead pigs, cattle, and sheep ashore should first apply to the rendering plant for a dead animal permit to avoid misunderstanding by the water and land police. (Article 11) If the dead pigs, cattle, and sheep sent to the plant for rendering every day cannot be completely rendered, and the total number of those left accounts for two-thirds of the number of the first rendering, night work must be done to catch up with the rendering. The foreman and helpers will be subsidized with four jiao (cents) for night work meals per person. (Article 12) The oil, skin, bone residue, intestines, and other items rendered from dead pigs, cattle, and sheep will be tendered by the plant, and the winning bidder should handle them in accordance with the regulations of the Health Bureau. (Article 13) In addition to presiding over the affairs of the entire plant under the direction of the responsible officer, the veterinary technician should fill out and submit a daily report on the rendering of dead animals to the bureau. (Article 14) The methods of reward and punishment for the staff of each plant shall be in accordance with the rules of reward and punishment for the staff of the municipal government. (Article 15) If there are any matters not covered in these detailed rules, they may be submitted to the municipal government for revision. (Article 16) These detailed rules shall be implemented from the date of approval by the municipal government.

Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau's Regulations for the Animal Carcass Rendering Plant 142

(Approved and promulgated on September 25, Year 19)

(Article 1) This plant is affiliated to the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau and is responsible for rendering animal carcasses and all related matters. (Article 2) This plant shall have one veterinary technician, one accountant and administrator, and other staff members may be hired or transferred at any time depending on the complexity of the affairs. (Article 3) The veterinary technician of this plant shall, under the direction of the director of the bureau and the head of the responsible section, manage all affairs of the entire plant. (Article 4) The accountant and administrator of this plant shall, under the direction of the veterinary technician, handle all accounting and administrative matters of the entire plant. (Article 5) The staff of this plant shall, under the direction of the veterinary technician, handle the investigation of dead animals and other matters. (Article 6) The detailed rules for the operation of this plant shall be formulated separately. (Article 7) If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, the Health Bureau may submit them to the municipal government for revision. (Article 8) These regulations shall be implemented from the date of submission to the municipal government for approval.

Educational News Highlights

Jiangsu Education Finance Committee Meeting 143

Concrete measures to reorganize education fees and tax revenues. All agencies must raise sufficient funds to pay off debts within ten days. Request the Provincial Government to order county finance bureaus not to misappropriate funds. The Jiangsu Education Finance Committee, urgently needing to discuss measures to address the continued arrears in education fees for this year, convened a meeting at the Education Department at 3:00 PM on the 1st of this month. Committee members Wu Zhihui, Niu Tiesheng, Ye Chucang, Chen Hexian, Zhang Naiyan, Wang Maozu, Liu Zhiwei, Gao Yang, Ma Ketan, and others attended the meeting in full. Minister Jiang of the Ministry of Education sent a representative, Wu Yan Yin, and Director Chen of the Finance Department also sent a representative. Chairman Niu reported that many important matters were decided during the discussions, which are summarized as follows: Regarding the reorganization of education fees and tax revenues, after detailed discussions by the committee members, concrete measures were developed. Regarding how to raise and allocate funds for the arrears in expenses for July, August, and September for provincial education institutions, it was generally agreed that the schools were in dire need of funds, and that it was essential to raise and allocate funds as soon as possible to meet the urgent needs. Therefore, it was resolved that the managing office should quickly borrow from banks and various counties and allocate the funds as soon as possible within ten days, and that in order to take into account the most urgent needs of the schools, a portion of the funds should be raised and allocated within three days. It was also agreed to nominate Director Chen of the Finance Department, President Zhang of the Central University, and Director Chen of the Education Department to jointly negotiate. Furthermore, as there were still cases of misappropriation of funds among counties, even though the division of education funds had been implemented, it was resolved that the Education Department should consult with the Provincial Government and the Finance Department to order the county finance bureaus not to misappropriate any education funds, regardless of the item of expenditure, and to strictly implement the division of grain transport fees. In addition, regarding the two vacancies for inspectors, it was resolved to appoint Qi Yong and Ren Zhongmin to fill the positions. In many counties, the salt tax was not divided in the same way as the grain transport fees. It was resolved to request the Finance Department to issue a notice to the county finance bureaus to divide the funds in accordance with the grain transport fees. There were many other important matters, which cannot all be recorded. The meeting adjourned after 9:00 PM. Committee members Wu Zhihui and Niu Tiesheng made time to come from Nanjing to Zhenjiang to preside over the meeting, as it was of great importance. They immediately returned to Nanjing that night, but as the meeting adjourned too late, they had to take the Shanghai-Nanjing overnight train back this morning. During the meeting, all committee members were unusually spirited.

Joint Meeting of Ministries and the Academy Regarding Foreigners Coming to China for Scientific Research 144

The Academia Sinica and the Ministries of Interior, Foreign Affairs, Military Affairs, Politics, Education, and other ministries held a joint meeting on the 2nd at 10:00 AM at the Ministry of Education regarding foreigners coming to China for scientific research. Those present included Li Huaying of the Ministry of Military Affairs, Xu Shoushang of the Academia Sinica, Wu Sishan of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Zhu Ying of the Ministry of Interior, Liu Mingxun of the Ministry of Interior, Chen Shizhen of the Ministry of Education, Zhu Baoqin of the Ministry of Education, Peng Baichuan of the Ministry of Education. The meeting was chaired by Chen Shizhen. The Chairman reported that the Ministry of Education had recently received notifications from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs regarding foreign organizations intending to come to China for research, including: (1) Robert B. Ekelberry and others from the United States going to Xinjiang to conduct scientific research; (2) Rickmers of Germany bringing weapons to Xinjiang to measure and study glaciers and geological resources; and (3) Smith of the United States bringing weapons to Yunnan and Guizhou provinces to investigate animals. The opinions of the Academia Sinica and the Peiping Antiquities Preservation Committee had been sought, and both had responded (details omitted). However, as these foreigners are going deep into the interior for scientific research, which is of great importance to the country, it is necessary to discuss appropriate measures carefully in order to respect sovereignty. Therefore, the Academia Sinica and relevant ministries were invited to meet to develop a proper plan. The points to be discussed today are approximately two: (1) Whether or not the above three cases should be allowed to enter the country for research; (2) If they are allowed to enter the country, what conditions should be set? Please express your opinions.

Results of the discussion: (1) The case of Robert B. Ekelberry and others from the United States going to Xinjiang for scientific research and the case of Rickmers of Germany bringing weapons to Xinjiang to measure and study glaciers and geological resources were discussed together and it was answered that they should be postponed temporarily. The reason is that the existing Northwest Scientific Expedition Team is conducting a survey in Xinjiang and has not yet completed it. After the team completes the survey and reports the results, a plan will be determined. (2) The case of Smith and others from the Chicago Museum of Natural History organizing an animal survey was approved for entry, and the conditions were to be decided by the Academia Sinica and the Ministry of Education. However, before entering the country, the following items must be notified to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for transfer and compliance: 1. The team must first submit a detailed plan for animal research (the areas passed through, the round-trip route, etc. must be explained) and send it through the embassy to the government for review by the competent authorities. 2. A brief list of the number of team members. 3. Weapons are allowed to be carried according to the number opened in the previous letter from the American Minister James, but the passport must be verified by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and transferred to the Ministry of Military Affairs for approval to issue a license to carry weapons. 4. Surveying equipment is not allowed to be carried. 5. China sends personnel to participate in the survey. 6. Half of the collected specimens shall belong to China for commemoration. The only item without a duplicate shall be left to China. After the team signs all the conditions, the Yunnan and Guizhou provincial governments should be consulted for verification before entering the country. (3) Regarding the matters of foreigners coming to China to conduct scientific research in the future, the Academia Sinica and the Ministry of Education will formulate unified measures, and then invite relevant ministries to meet and pass them.

Death of Section Chief Rong of the Ministry of Education 145

Rong Weiyang, section chief of the Fourth Section of the General Affairs Department of the Ministry of Education, was a native of Wuxi and was 39 years old. He previously served as the principal of an overseas Chinese middle school in Nanyang and was enthusiastic and devoted to overseas Chinese affairs. In the autumn of the 17th year of the Republic, he was appointed section chief of the Ministry of Education. He was honest and hardworking. Recently, he suffered from typhoid fever, which the doctor failed to diagnose, and passed away on the 29th of last month. His funeral was simple. All colleagues in the Ministry of Education plan to hold a memorial service around the middle of this month, and his family will hold a funeral in a month or two.

The Future of Chinese Tennis – Qiu Feihai 152

Talent Emerges, Emphasis on Practice

As Mr. Qiu Feihai, a Chinese tennis national athlete, is about to tour Europe, he has specially written "The Future of Chinese Tennis," based on his observations, to be published in this newspaper. It is recorded below. Since the 8th Far Eastern Games held in 1926, lawn tennis in China has made rapid progress. Currently, it has become one of the most popular sports in various universities and amateur sports circles. Tennis clubs have been established one after another, and their number is not small. The large number of spectators at each competition is enough to show the enthusiasm of the Chinese people for this sport. The China National Amateur Athletic Federation has also been organizing various competitions every year, promoting and encouraging them with all its might. Looking at the rate of progress in recent years, it is not difficult to believe that China will soon be able to compete with others in the world of tennis.

At present, our country has many promising young tennis players, such as Zheng Zhaojia of St. John's University, Yu Tianguang of Shanghai University, and countless other strong players that I have seen in previous competitions. In the near future, they will all stand out in the tennis world and win glory for the country. These players all have the potential to win championships, what they need is experience, which can be gained by participating in more competitions and competing with those who are better than them. This sport should be started at a young age, and beginners should pay attention to the accuracy of their grip, stance, and stroke. It is advisable to first ask for guidance from famous coaches, or read more of the works of world tennis master Tilden, and then start practicing. If you have no idea about these three, please do not try it lightly, because once you go astray, it will be difficult to turn back, and only a small fraction of those who can correct it later will succeed. If you can follow the correct posture from the beginning, and then practice without interruption, you will definitely become a good tennis player. However, if you want to surpass others, it still depends on your talent, because tennis is not just about hitting the ball, but also requires a soft touch, courage, patience, strength, and strategy.

Japanese tennis has now surpassed all other countries in the Far East and is comparable to world-class players. The reason why they have reached this position is largely due to the encouragement and support of their people, providing various conveniences to young players. For example, universities and other sports centers all have good tennis courts, which is of great benefit to the progress of their skills. If they are always confined to poor tennis courts, it will lead to bad habits in their strokes and timing. In addition, their sports organizations encourage competitions between clubs, send teams to visit overseas, and invite world-famous players to perform in Japan for learning purposes, all of which are aimed at promoting rapid progress in tennis skills.

Chinese tennis is still in its infancy, but looking at the remarkable progress in recent years and the efforts of the China National Amateur Athletic Federation to encourage competitions, it is expected that first-class talents who will win world tennis championships will be produced in the future.

A Laughing Matter 160

— Hai Ke

Patient: Doctor, do you think my illness is serious?

Doctor: It depends on your daily life to determine if you smoke.

Patient: I don't smoke.

Doctor: Do you drink?

Patient: I don't drink.

Doctor: Do you dance?

Patient: I don't like to dance.

Doctor: Then you must visit brothels and gamble.

Patient: No, no, I have always hated prostitution and gambling.

Doctor: Poor man. Then what are you going to do after you get well?

Grandfather: Child, I don't approve of you putting on powder and rouge, dressing up so seductively. You must know that artificial is never as good as natural.

Granddaughter: Grandfather, I don't agree with your words. For example, what about the false teeth you wear?

A: Last night, I got drunk and went home in the rain. I made a fool of myself.

B: What happened?

A: When I got home in the middle of the night, I put a wet umbrella in the quilt and slept with my wife. I squatted on the umbrella stand all night myself.

Thrilling Speedway Racing at Weile Garden 161

— Cheng Zhizheng

The people of Shanghai often have a tendency to follow trends. No matter what it is, as long as it is new and interesting, once it is spread, everyone will flock to it. Circuses and crab-backed beauties have become a thing of the past. The most sensational thing now is the bicycle race at Weile Garden. The usually deserted Haig Road has been transformed into a place of bustling traffic. Last week, my friends and I also went to visit, and I felt that there were several points worth recording.

The Uniqueness of the Track The tracks of ordinary track and field competitions are flat, while the tracks of Weile Garden are sloped. The slope varies, some are 45 degrees, and some steep places are even about 70 degrees. All are made of thin wooden boards, which are exceptionally smooth. It is truly unique.

The Initiator's Martyrdom It is said that the initiator of Weile Garden was a Dutchman. He was able to ride extremely fast motorbikes on high-sloped tracks. But once, when he was testing his skills, because of the high speed, he involuntarily rushed up and fell from a height of more than thirty feet, and died.

The Referee Injured That day, there was a Japanese, a Chinese, and an Annamese competing in motorbike racing. In the last lap, everyone tried their best to drive fast. The Japanese saw that he was catching up with the Annamese. I don't know what carelessness it was, but the motorbike rolled straight down and happened to hit a Japanese referee. At that moment, the person's face turned pale and he fell to the ground unable to speak. The person in the car was also injured.

Dangerously Crushed This kind of racing is indeed very dangerous. When it comes to the thrilling moment, everyone really sweats for them. Once, three Westerners competed in motorbikes. I don't know what happened, but the car suddenly left the body and the person fell on the track. Taking advantage of the situation, he also fell several feet away. He quickly climbed down. Fortunately, a car came from behind like a whirlwind. If he was only one second late leaving the track, he would have been crushed. How dangerous! However, this Westerner, although injured from the fall, still got up and drove around the track. His spirit of a strong man is admirable after all. The audience gave a full house of applause.

Particularly Fat Body Most of the actors are very fat. Later, I found out that it was to prevent falls. So they put some soft things inside their clothes. There were also things to protect the head, so they felt particularly swollen. It was only finished at five o'clock.

Cheng Yanqiu and Wang Shaolou 162

— Master Kan Yun Lou

When I was young, I watched Huiban operas. There was no such thing as a grand finale or a grand finale. There was no such thing as a lead role or a supporting role. There was also no such thing as a headliner or a second-rate acrobat who played a dragon. (Although there is this term for playing a dragon, good actors often take on the role.) But in Beijing operas, the boundaries are clear and the status is very different. This is even more so today. The cooperation between Mei and Yang, and the cooperation between Yu and Yang, cannot last for long. Mei and Yu cannot be seen in joint performances except for private shows. Even second-rate old men are unwilling to be vassals of female roles. And second-rate female roles are also unwilling to be attendants of old men. Therefore, in recent years, the flat-rate south tour has failed because they cannot carry a suitable supporting role. Even if he is as virtuous as Shu Yan, his plays such as "Visiting Mother and Assassinating Tang" are still not popular because the listeners have the regret of only being able to listen to half of the play.

Cheng Yanqiu has toured Shanghai and has achieved good results. The two words "Cheng cavity" are enough to be immortal alongside Tan's tune. However, the people who sing Cheng cavity today only sing a few plays such as "Scolding the Palace" and "Golden Lock Record". I have not seen anyone imitate his "Wujiapo", "Fenhe Bay", "Mulberry Garden Meeting", "Imperial Stele Pavilion", and "Lotus Lantern". I don't know that Yanqiu has made careful studies on these plays. However, "Scolding the Palace" and "Golden Lock" are solo plays for Qingyi, so listeners will naturally be pleased. The Fenhe and Mulberry Garden plays emphasize both Sheng and Dan roles. When Yanqiu performed in the past, the old men were not up to par, so the good points were all overshadowed. Therefore, those who talk about Cheng cavity only know about "Scolding the Palace", "Golden Lock", and "Wenji Returning to Han".

Yanqiu once co-starred with Shuyan in "Visiting Mother and Assassinating Tang" at Gongwu Stage. The popularity was unprecedented. It can be seen that with proper matching, any play can be attractive. Yanqiu and Shuyan both have creations in the opera world and have similar status. The tunes of the two are also very suitable. I often think to myself that if Yanqiu and Shuyan can cooperate for a long time, they will definitely be able to promote many old plays. However, in reality, it is impossible to realize. Now Shuyan is ill and has not been on stage for a long time. Those who love Yu's tune only tend to Wang Shaolou. He has not been on stage for a long time. He is young, talented, and beautiful. He imitates Shuyan in singing and acting and can get his spirit. This time, following Yanqiu to the south, not only the plays "Qionglin Feast", "Losing Jieting", "Dingjun Mountain", and "Nanyang Pass" will be enough to satisfy the people of Shanghai, but also "Wujiapo", "Fenhe Bay", "Lotus Lantern", and "Imperial Stele Pavilion" can add to Yanqiu's brilliance. Cheng and Yu's cooperation, this wish is ultimately empty. Having Shaolou as a match is already satisfactory. Peonies and green leaves complement each other. I am deeply pleased for Yanqiu to have found someone. The Mulberry Garden and Fenhe plays will become popular all over the world from now on. It is also a good phenomenon for the revival of old plays.

Talking About Crabs 163

— Bai Gui

In the clear autumn, the crabs are fat and the flowers are yellow. It is the time to hold a crab and drink wine. The Nanjing Road World Show is in line with the times, and there is a display of crab-backed beauties for people to watch, which is a feast for the eyes. The people in Shanghai can see what they have never seen before. What a happy thing it is. It is a pity that the crab beauty is too small in size. Although she has a beautiful face, the viewers are not clear about it. It is a pity to cover up the beauty. If it can be covered with a microscope and magnified, then the true face of Mount Lu will be in sight.

The world is so big that there is nothing strange. Is it just revealing a crab beauty? In my opinion, there are two strange crabs. One, in Hengzhou East Township, there are crabs as big as washbasins. Whenever it rains, they roam the ridges and fields. They are covered with hairy whiskers, and their backs are green. They are not seen when the weather is clear. At first, some villagers caught them, but their hands were stabbed by the whiskers and the pain was like a knife cut. They had to release them and the pain stopped. Therefore, they respected them as divine crabs. According to the elders, it is said that they heard from their ancestors that this crab has lived for more than five hundred years and has seen all the vicissitudes of life. Now no one dares to catch them, and so on. In 1926, the Revolutionary Army marched north. Some soldiers stationed in Dongxiang saw the crabs and killed them with bayonets, cooked them and ate them. Their taste was extremely fresh, which was beyond the reach of ordinary crabs. Alas, the five-hundred-year-old crab was actually killed by soldiers. What a misfortune! One was in the suburbs of Suzhou. I went for a walk with my friend Xu Zibu. Where the green grass moved, a crab walked out horizontally. At first, I thought it was an ordinary crab. Then I saw that when it moved, its feet stretched upwards and hugged its waist tightly. Xu Zibu smiled and said, "This is a dancing crab." This crab has horns about an inch long on its head. The horns are now in four colors: yellow, white, black, and red, which are dazzling. I wanted to catch it and take it back for appreciation. Xu Zibu was very superstitious and said that since things have strange appearances, they must have the attachment of gods. So I didn't catch it. The above two crabs and the crab beauty displayed in the New World can be called three strange crabs.

In the past, a certain tycoon had a crab recipe that described the method of cooking crabs in forty-six kinds. Unfortunately, I am forgetful. If I can remember the details and write them down here, it will definitely be what the gluttons want to hear. I only remember one section: use crab roe to cook cabbage and seep chicken soup. Its taste is rich and refreshing.

New Knowledge of the Family 165

— Tian Xu Wo Sheng Editor

As soon as the autumn wind rises, ordinary people's skin feels dry, mostly due to anemia. The skin lacks fat nourishment, so you can apply milk and borax glycerin, which is very effective. However, milk is very easy to spoil, so it is better to use Invincible brand Butterfly Cream, because Butterfly Cream is made of milk cool, does not contain alkalinity, and can absorb the nourishing ingredients in the air to moisturize the skin, so it can avoid chapped skin and stop itching, which is very effective. As for internal blood tonics, Invincible brand grape juice or wine is the most suitable.

The skin of women and children is extremely delicate and is easily damaged by wind and sun, so they often apply powder for protection, just like houses are painted and walls are plastered. It is certain that those who are painted and plastered will last longer and stay new than those who are not painted and plastered. It is also to protect the weak nature of the content, increase the appearance, and facilitate washing away dust and resisting wind and sun. The method is very good. However, the face powder in ancient times was made by burning lead and tin. There are three types of lead: one is white lead, translated as zinc, the second is blue lead, translated as bismuth, and the third is black lead, directly translated as lead. Among the three, black lead is the cheapest and easily oxidized. When made into lead powder, it turns black when exposed to magnets, so it is harmful to the skin. Western face powder is all made of zinc white, while Eastern face powder is made of blue lead. If you test it with sulfuric acid, you can easily distinguish it. Those that do not change color are not harmful to the skin. Invincible brand blue box powder is zinc white, and yellow box powder is added with bismuth. It is delicate and ironed, which is better than lead powder. This is due to the proper combination, so its advantages are comparable to the face powder of the East and West, and it is truly a good product among skin protectors. Its usage is to apply Butterfly Cream first and then apply powder, so it will not fall off or stick, which is completely different from ordinary greases and vulgar powders.

Once the pocket mirror box powder imported from the West is used up, it is often impossible to add more. You can mail it to the Family Industry Agency on Guohuo Road in Shanghai to ask for a match, but attach a three-cent stamp. If the size is two inches in diameter, the agency has ready-made ones for sale, named "Invincible Brand Matching Powder", which sells for only two cents. All department stores sell it. There is also a small aluminum box with a silk puff, which can also be used directly. However, when transferring it to the mirror box, take out the powder pan. The empty box can also be used for other purposes.

The Deeds of Mr. Zhao Tieqiao (I) 166

— Zhao Guangzu

The China Merchants Bureau is handling the funeral for my late father. Guangzu and others will accompany my mother and uncle to escort the coffin back to Sichuan to be buried next to the ancestral graves. Because senior members of various revolutionary movements inquired about my late father's deeds, I recount them with tears. It is said that when my late father was over ten years old, he and my late aunt's husband, Huang Lusheng, and Yang Shenyou, were known as the "Three Heroes of Yongning." They were indignant at the corruption of the Qing government and plotted to overthrow it. Yongning was located deep in the mountains, and Sichuan was rife with bandits. The gatherings in Yongning were especially large. The three of them traveled in the mountains, befriending their leaders. Five years before the founding of the Republic of China, Mr. Xiong Fan and Mr. Huang Fusheng were ordered by Sun Yat-sen, the leader of the Tongmenghui (Revolutionary Alliance), to plan for Sichuan. Shenyou, my aunt's husband, returned from Japan after studying police work. My late father also returned from Chengdu after transferring from Xulu Middle School to Ziliujing Shuren School. He and Lusheng, my aunt's husband, had both joined the Tongmenghui. Xiong and Huang had already met Shenyou, my aunt's husband, and then together they visited Lusheng, my aunt's husband, and all came to Jin'e Pond to meet my late father. They spoke in secret for days, intending to start an uprising in Yongning. The Yong and Mi factions could not agree, so they established a Youth Association to resolve the issue, explaining the revolution to them. The mountain armies were all happy to hear it. At that time, Mr. Yang Cangbai was the principal of Yongning Middle School, providing chemical products to Mr. Fusheng to make bombs. The medicine exploded, injuring Mr. Fusheng's hand and eye. The matter was somewhat leaked. The county magistrate sent a message saying, "Leave quickly, or you will be arrested." On the ninth day of the ninth month, my late father and more than ten comrades climbed a high mountain, entered a deep forest, slaughtered a cow, brewed wine, drew their swords, struck the ground, and sang and shouted all day before leaving.

They arrived in Luzhou. Because there were many party members in southeastern Sichuan, they wanted to occupy Jiang'an and connect with Yongning, leading the mountain armies out. They planned to attack Luzhou and then go east to Chongqing. It was decided to attack Jiang'an on September 30th. My late father traveled to a neighboring county to meet with party members in Shangjiang, forming the Tieshan (Iron Mountain) organization. My late father and Mr. Cheng Defan were appointed as commanders of Jiang'an. On September 27th, my late father, carrying ten bombs from Tieshan, passed through Yibin, obtained military tickets and a party flag, and rushed into Jiang'an city. Upon arrival, he ordered that a fire be set inside the east gate at midnight. Several hundred patrolmen from Zhenwu Mountain attacked the east gate, and over a thousand bandits attacked the west gate. At midnight, the fire illuminated the sky, and gunfire erupted outside the city. The city was in chaos. My late father and Mr. Cheng stayed in an inn, drafting proclamations and sorting out bombs, believing that the city would fall. They intended to arm themselves and rush out. Officials and soldiers wandered to the inn. Realizing that the situation was about to fail, they firmly held the bombs and sat on the bed, watching for officials and soldiers to enter, intending to throw the bombs and die with them. Officials and soldiers knocked on the door, and they calmly replied, "I am a student. Is the fire extinguished? Why is there gunfire?" The soldiers said, "The fire is about to be extinguished. Don't worry, it's just bandits attacking the city." They did not suspect that the city was being attacked by party members under the command of the two men. They searched the adjacent houses and left. At dawn, our army was defeated. They rushed out of the city and went to Luzhou. After having a meal, they fled to Longchang and hid in a coal pit in Tianle Mountain for more than ten days before returning to Yongning.

European Travel Correspondence (76) 167

— Liu Haisu

Diary of a Pilgrimage to Italy

(2) En Route

The two of us chatted about many trivial things. The other three were all sound asleep. Looking out the window at the sky, I saw only the starry sky, still shimmering tirelessly above. The bumping and jarring of the train played a monotonous tune in the extremely quiet realm. Time passed easily. Before I knew it, it was already dawn. At S station, we got off the train to eat some coffee and bread. From then on, the scenery was very good all the way. By noon, we reached Lake Annecy and Lake Bourget. This is where the French poet Lamartine wrote the poem "The Lake" and fell in love a hundred years ago. Along the way, the verdant and beautiful hills gradually turned into towering mountains. The rushing torrents roared incessantly. How many miles we traveled then, I can't remember. The shape of the clouds, the light of the sun, the temperature of the climate, and everything else gradually changed. From Meana onwards, our train was winding through majestic valleys. This is the highest peak of the Alps. Hundreds of miles of snow-covered peaks, with a momentum of tens of millions, rise straight into the clouds. This is the world-famous Mont Blanc. Mont Blanc is such a beautiful name, such a grand place name. It is so white and so high. White. It is truly untouched by a single speck of dust. High. It is high in a meaningful way. There are peaks beyond the clouds, and peaks on top of peaks. My heart truly envies its whiteness and height. (Mont Blanc is 4,810 meters high, equivalent to 10,000 feet.) Although there are also graceful clouds covering and winding around it, and raging winds invading it, the air it enjoys is ultimately different. It is still so white and so high. This sublime and wonderful realm is completely natural. There is simply nothing you can do about it. You can only look up at it. But I was the only one gazing up at it from the window, not wanting to miss a single moment. If I had the chance to live in this desolate valley and fully enjoy it, I might be able to produce abundant and beautiful works. I truly think so. I have traveled to Mount Tai, Mount Hua, and Mount Heng, but they are ultimately not as majestic as these hundreds of miles of white peaks piercing the clouds, or as open and bright. Back then, Napoleon led his troops, stepped over Mont Blanc, and entered Italy with such spirit. His great footprints can still make people imagine and be amazed.

Slight Rise in Financial Specie Market 168

Small Fluctuations, Transactions Evened Out

Yesterday, the situation in the specie market on the fourth was peaceful, with a slight potential for a rise. However, there were no major changes. The total difference was only two or three taels. As for foreign exchange, it was strong in the morning and weak in the afternoon. Banks were selling, and the intentions of other firms seemed high, but transactions were not idle. However, there were no large amounts. This was probably because the banks would close on the sixth of this month, and the gold market would also be closed for one day. Therefore, most people were just evening out their positions. For example, Yongfeng, Yuancheng Yong, and hedgers were all taking deliveries, while Da, Taikangrun, and Richang, among others, were generally selling. The market saw a high surge early in the day because it was rumored that the United States had a lot of silver bars to supply. Although the price went up, the market situation was very soft, and people's hearts were uneasy. Afterwards, the market fluctuated slightly by one or two taels. Then, because sellers were eager to sell and the market atmosphere was not good, rumors suddenly arose that government bonds were falling. As a result, the market turned sharply downwards and plummeted to just over sixty-three taels. Until the final outcome, Yuan Maoyong and others chased after the market, suddenly pulling it up by more than one tael, to above sixty-four taels. In the afternoon, because it was the weekend, the market was closed according to regulations.

The opening price of the November specie market was 565.4 taels, an increase of 2.1 taels. However, British silver bars rose another three-sixteenths, and American silver also rose one-quarter. Afterwards, there were divergent opinions among the clerks, so there was an upward and downward movement of more than one tael, fluctuating around 66 taels. There was not much change in drafts. The December American gold was traded between Japanese banks at 39.5 taels. Mitsui had offered to sell the next month's Japanese gold at 1 tael 2 qian 6 fen to 1 tael 2 qian 5 fen 7.5 hao. Flour Prices Near and Far are Firm 178

Yesterday in the flour market, after the opening bell in both the morning and afternoon, prices for all months showed a trend of being firm in both the near and far terms. This month, due to sluggish actual sales and the large number of warehouse receipts from previous months that have not yet been fully sold, the bulls cannot avoid being cautious. It seems that the warehouse receipts to come in the future still appear considerable, given the high market prices. However, for the far-term months, market sentiment has stabilized. As the price of foreign wheat continues to rise by two or three dimes to seven or eight dimes, sales are rare, and the market naturally shows vitality. Moreover, the inverted price structure will be difficult to sustain when supply and demand even out in the future. The shift in market sentiment is not without reason. As a result, this month's price is up by a small 0.025 tael compared to the previous day, November and December are up by 0.1 tael, January/February is up by 0.075 tael, and March is up by 0.125 tael.

Reasons for the Stabilization of Wheat Futures 179

The continued rise in foreign wheat prices led to hedging in the wheat futures market yesterday. After the opening bell in both the morning and afternoon, prices for all months generally stabilized. As the quotations for foreign wheat continued to rise, many large short sellers engaged in hedging for November and December. For the far-term months, speculative shorts gradually covered their positions based on foreign wheat quotations, and inland dealers also followed suit, causing the market to improve across the board. The market situation has reached a point where it needs to temporarily consolidate and observe the trend. As a result, this month's price is up by 0.1 tael compared to the previous day, November is up by 0.3 tael, December is up by 0.1 tael, January/February is up by 0.2 tael, and March is unchanged. The spot wheat market is such that manufacturers and dealers are willing to trade only after a method is agreed upon for inspecting inventory and bearing costs.

Straight tribute flannel was shipped in large quantities to Wanbei Zhenjiang and other ports, reportedly due to additional taxes. Yesterday, Moganshan was priced at 0.32 tael, Lieyan at 0.325 tael, and Shuangtonglu at 0.2925 tael, with over 100 pieces shipped out. Western goods were even quieter, and bleached cloth was rarely inquired about as the season ended. The asking prices for Yuanchou Taixi satin were too high, making it difficult to sell.

Metals: Black Sheet Iron Prices Increase by 0.25 tael 186

Ten sheets of black sheet iron increased in price by 0.25 tael yesterday and were sold for 10.075 taels. It is said that the recent supply has been extremely tight, while demand from various regions has been strong, resulting in a lack of inventory in the market. It is also said that Yingkou, Niuzhuang, and other regions have recently been making more purchases, so prices may rise further in the future.

Sugar Market: Sales of New Coarse White Sugar Still Active 187

Yesterday's sugar market reports from producing regions showed that the price of Cuban spot sugar was 1.03125, down 0.0625 from the previous report. New York sugar futures were priced at 1.07 for December, 1.18 for March next year, 1.25 for May, and 1.38 for September, up by 0.01 tael, except for May, which was unchanged. The buying interest in coarse white sugar from the guild remained quiet, with new goods selling briskly at 8 taels, while old goods saw little interest at 7.8 taels. No. 20 medium white sugar was priced at 7.75 taels, No. 18 at 7.7 taels, and No. 10 Dutch red sugar at 6.55 taels. Due to the surge in arrivals, the market was generally flat and sluggish. Transactions in Japanese sugar were also limited, with N mark at 8 taels, 　mark at 8.125 taels, YT mark at 7.85 taels, and YP mark at 8 taels. Demand was weak, and the market was depressed. The exchange offered its own ice flower green sugar, with the price remaining at the original 7.6 taels, and the market remained firm.

Book and Newspaper Introduction

Expansion Monthly Second Issue 206

By Yang Shaozhi

Edited by the Expansion Literary Society

Since June 1st of this year, when Nationalist literary movement participants gathered in Shanghai and issued a declaration, a roar of protest has risen in literary circles. In the current era, where both old and new literature have declined, it seems a life-saving force has emerged, rescuing the dying literary world's crisis and paving the way for its progress. Their representative publication, the Vanguard Weekly, was thus born. It has now been published up to its seventeenth issue. Many have already introduced its rich content and solid theoretical base, so there is naturally no need for me to bother. Although it is a publication with limited capacity, it has already generated sufficient power. Following this, the most diligent Nationalist literary movement was naturally in Nanjing. This is not surprising, considering Nanjing is where Jiangnan scholars gather, and it is also the capital of the Republic of China. Therefore, the literary circles of Nanjing, with convenient transportation and a fondness for literature, easily accepted the emerging literary movement, realizing that only the literature needed in the current state of China could save the declining state of Chinese literature. Consequently, many Nationalist literary groups in Nanjing sprang up like bamboo shoots after rain, and Nationalist literary publications bloomed like bursting buds.

"Expansion" is such a publication of the times. It has recently been published to its second issue. In the second issue, there are five original works, four of which are novels and one a play. In addition, there is a translated novel, an article on popular drama, and an article discussing "The National Consciousness Expressed in Shandong Folk Songs."

Bearing the banner of a Nationalist literary publication, logically, every creation should naturally reveal its national character. Nationalist literary movement participants once told us in the inaugural issue of Vanguard Weekly that the characteristics of Nationalist literature are "powerful, hopeful, bright, willful, and spiritual. It should awaken national consciousness, inspire national vitality, and unite to fight for the nation." However, in "Expansion," we rarely find these characteristics, which inevitably leaves us with some disappointment amidst our welcome. This is, of course, too harsh a criticism, but it can also be said that our love is too intense. I hope the editors of "Expansion" can forgive my nitpicking, and at the same time, I also hope the editors of "Expansion" will pay more attention to this aspect, clearly reveal our central consciousness, and intensify the responsibility of awakening national consciousness.

"The National Consciousness Expressed in Shandong Folk Songs" is an article by Lou Zikuang reading Gu Qizhong's compilation "Collection of Shandong Folk Songs." From it, he gathered several items expressing unique national consciousness and formed this article. Folk songs are originally national, and adding some national consciousness to them naturally makes them Nationalist literature. The suffering of the Shandong people has long been subject to the ravages of warlords, and they often encounter the frequent poisoning of red and white imperialists. Under the ravages, they naturally have to struggle for their own survival, and under the oppression, they naturally have to issue painful groans for their own survival. Therefore, in their folk songs, they also try their best to reveal the call to overthrow imperialists and eliminate the remaining warlords. There are indeed several of them that I think are remarkable. Let me introduce all the ones about overthrowing imperialists and eliminating warlords:

(1) Folk songs about hating imperialists

Advise compatriots,

Remember firmly,

The May 3rd massacre is no small matter,

Sever economic ties with Japan,

Never forget it – Shandong Zhangqiu

(2) Folk songs about eliminating the remaining warlords

One two three four five,

Attack Jinan Prefecture,

First kill Zhang Zongchang,

Then kill Chu Yupu,

First there were the Boxers,

Then there were the Red Lanterns,

Touched the telegraph pole,

Killed Zhang Zongchang,

Only then woke up to peace! | Shandong Ningyang

In short, I think these kinds of folk songs are worth introducing. I further hope that departments in various places can record and publicize this type of folk song as much as possible.

The insults that overseas Chinese suffer in foreign countries are naturally the result of our Chinese nation being old and incompetent. The situation of these insults is almost equivalent to the pain encountered in the Miao dens occupied by irrational barbarians. If it were completely and thoroughly recorded, I am afraid it would really be infuriating. The article "Returning to the Country" depicts a scene of the insults suffered by overseas Chinese. Can we accept the elegant name of "dirty yellow"? Friends, the time has come, ignite our national emotions, join a just and bright organization, and work together for the nation!

In the old society, the concept of moral teaching不知道葬送了多少有爲的靑年男女, the play "The Death of the Fengxin" is about a promising young man who was活活地被社會排擠得不容其生存. He died under the 名敎. It is a fact. A widow and orphan who cannot maintain their lives, while she got a man, maintaining their lives, has been in the spirit of three-day-long. She takes care of her own life and happiness, and she also takes care of the future of the orphans. She remarried. Is this action worth cursing? She woke up, she boldly冒天下的不大韙 and did this thing that people can't do. But the fact is even more unexpected. I want to curse the ruthlessness of the old society. The old society is toounforgiving to people. Because of her mother's remarriage, even this orphan was associated with being despised by society forever, and was constantly排擠 by society with惡辣手叚, causing him to sacrifice in the old society. The桔桎 of etiquette is too binding. Are we willing to be conquered綿羊, or are we willing to be sinners in 名敎? Awakened young people, come and work hard to break the堅壁 of 名敎 and save promising compatriots!

Also, the article "Random Talks on Popular Drama" is worth reading. The remaining articles inevitably still have the atmosphere of romance and decay. If these articles were published in literary publications, they might be worth appreciating. In Nationalist literary publications, it seems they should not have a place.

In short, in the two issues already published, "Expansion" does not yet have much substantial theory or enthusiastic and powerful creations. However, at least they have recognized the bright path. Future success can naturally also be predicted. May the gardeners bravely and carefully work hard together to cultivate this newly expanded garden and irrigate these buds that have not yet bloomed, in order to obtain a rich and fulfilling harvest!

Embellishments 207

— Wen Hua

Dusting Off the Lotus

Originally, in our old and vast China, riddled with sores, the toxins of the old society were deeply rooted in the stubborn hearts of people, especially in those remote and backward places. Due to inconvenient transportation or various other factors, even though it is now the so-called "20th century," they stubbornly maintain the full-blown old-fashioned habits of the old and young conservatives. Around them, it seems as if there is an iron wall that is difficult to break through, and they rarely accept modern culture. Even if there is some input, it will be hindered by the evils of the old society and suffer from indigestion. In name, China is already a country that has undergone revolutionary baptism, and at least those corrupt and old forces should be eradicated. However, if we calmly examine the facts, we will be greatly disappointed, just like the few witty satirical words described by the author of this book:

"...The Temple of Guan Yu... The walls are covered with broken and scattered colorful paper slogans, leaving traces of the so-called mass rally (!) three months ago, remnants of the declining theocratic era, as if wearing a multicolored fashionable dress."

In fact, in these places, revolution is just a show of changing the soup but not the medicine. Some old low-ranking officials of the seventh rank and old conservatives who retreated from the Qing Dynasty, or newly emerged fierce dog heads, just need to put on a revolutionary (!) coat over their rotten and stinky bodies, and they will immediately ascend the dragon gate and their value will increase tenfold. Then they can take advantage of their power and oppress the people, truly deserving the name of public bandits. Under their coercion, there are even some scholars and inferior runners, and the old etiquette relies entirely on these people to maintain it, so it can openly exist in the world. Once one or two young people with blood dare to confront them slightly, they can add the label of "traitor," which is even more powerful than violating the law, without any hesitation, and do whatever they want. This is an old trick they often use. Under this electric-grid-like tyranny, I don't know how many young people have been sacrificed.

Originally, some were bandit-scholars, but now that there is a revolution, they only need to wear a triangular belt, and they will transform themselves into revolutionary figures under the banner of the Blue Sky White Sun, and they can openly carry out their old tricks. There are indeed many kinds of tricks.

This kind of society really cannot tolerate good people. The general youth with blood are truly suffocated. Not only is love not free, but even slight anti-old remarks or actions must be careful about their heads. Under this heavy low pressure, the minds of young people are really bitter and depressed. The author of this book is someone who has suffered and been depressed in this environment. His wounded soul is now spread out before us with bloodstains. This is what we should thank him for. He has opened up a mental river for us, those who suffer from mental depression, a river that we want to vomit but cannot, and has boldly announced the crimes of the dog-headed society. How gratifying this is.

Cowardice seems to be the inferiority of our Chinese nation, especially the youth nowadays, who always muddle through things and dare not resist, only willing to submit. Therefore, the two sides of life cannot be unified, and there is constant contradiction in their minds. They clearly know that the environment is unreasonable, and they consciously feel that living in this environment is really unbearable. They often resent and curse the unsatisfactory reality, and at the same time, a new society grows in their ideals, which is completely different from the current one. The more they miss the ideal society, the more they hate reality, feeling that the surroundings are full of cruel, hypocritical, and deceitful creatures. So they think about fighting for their pitiful kind and against reality, feeling that they themselves are supremely sacred. However, no matter how beautiful your thoughts are, you can't stop the cynicism given by reality several times, and you will start to doubt, turn gray, and finally make you timid. In convenience, you will also compromise with reality, and as a result, you will be trapped in depression forever. Your conscience is permanently in heavy condemnation. The reality that you originally resolved to eliminate is still making a show of force around you, and the most sacred ideal society has become an illusion. Everything is attributed to fate, and you will even hate the ideal palace you once worshiped, forever dejected, indulging, and even dying.

The protagonist of this book, Wang Lie Feng, is a representative of this kind of person. He sees with his own eyes that his love rival is a heartless beast. He is the one who killed Wang Chun Sheng and burned the San Chun Xuan. He is the one who put the crimes he committed on the heads of kind farmers. He is the one who hung these kind and innocent farmers on the stove to make braised human flesh. His lover is also the fiancee of this beast, and he is also wrongly accused of being a communist bandit by him. He had previously said solemnly, "In order to liberate the suffering of all living beings, I will not hesitate to sacrifice myself," but he explained self-deceptively out of fear, "It was just an accidental fate, paired with such a thing. I had never resisted in the slightest, and at most I had stolen money and glared at the enemy a few times. I was already afraid that I was too rash." How ridiculous and contradictory this is. Later, when his lover was taken alive to Mei Ling to be buried by his beast-like fiancé, he did not go forward to save his brave lover and die with her. Instead, he retreated into the alley, just fainting in fear, and only shouting, "Go to Mei Ling, what else does the world have for me?"

This is the most pitiful person in the world. He is not at ease with reality, and he dare not resist it in the slightest. It would have been forgivable if he had been a sleepy-eyed person, but to be a rebel of conscience and a slave of the environment is truly an unforgivable sinner.

The author once said in his preface:

"When writing this little thing, my state of mind changed several times. At first, I sympathized with my protagonist Wang Lie Feng, pitying his dream of pursuing light. Gradually, I hated him. So I put a 'corpse's clothes' on him, letting him pass away in the cold wind. That can also be said to be hating myself, punishing my gray self."

It is very clear that the author has already taken on this responsibility. Wang Lie Feng is wearing a "corpse's clothes." Here, the author has already expressed himself, hating Wang Lie Feng and himself.

However, we cannot deny that this "corpse's clothes" is an unlucky thing. Therefore, I still hope that the author and himself will shout at the end of the preface,

"Light around, my efforts!

I am on my way again. I hope that a book is indeed partially successful in art. I believe that the author wrote his work with an honest heart, and there is not a single place where facts are fabricated and unrealistic. However, the layout has some flaws, and the scenes in each section cannot be tightly knit. The first section is a dynamic ending, which makes people stand up their hair, but the second section starts with a loose stillness, which seems a bit lax. It may not be without its shortcomings.

From the beginning of the first section to page eleven, I initially thought that the author was narrating the facts. In the middle of page eleven, it suddenly turned like this, "He couldn't think anymore..." It really confused me for a while. Later, I looked closely, and who knew that the above were all Lie Feng and her lover's memories standing by the bridge. This kind of arrangement is really not very beautiful and is also a small shortcoming of this book.

Bi Renyong, a teacher at the Chuangmen Cuiying Middle School in Suzhou, is proficient in agronomy. He recently translated Professor Cheng Zhitian's latest experimental poultry farming book into one volume, which is a must-read for poultry farmers. To request a copy, send two jiao for postage directly to the school.

The 14th volume, number 36 of the Bank Weekly, was published yesterday. The contents include discussions on prohibiting the import of Japanese silkworm cocoons, silver price talks (part 2), an overview of the post-war German banking system (part 2), minutes of the International League of Nations conference on the unification of bill of exchange laws (part 3), recent monetary and financial theories (part 8), reading about how to solve the difficulties of bank employee guarantors, and American newly revised tax regulations and China-U.S. trade, among other works.

Manuscript Guidelines for Book and Newspaper Introductions 209

(1) The text is limited to introducing the latest publications at home and abroad. In addition to literary works, all books and newspapers on politics, economics, law, science, education, etc., are included in the introduction, but books and newspapers without connections will not be introduced.

(2) Pictures are limited to recent works by new domestic and foreign artists and attached pictures related to the text.

(3) Texts on textual research and research on ancient Chinese books will not be published.

(4) Pictures and photos are limited to those related to the text.

(5) Each text should not exceed 3,000 words at most.

(6) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(7) Do not write the manuscript horizontally, and do not write in cursive script. Western text should be omitted where possible. If it is necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

(8) Do not draw pictures with blue ink, and do not use colored paper. White paper and black ink must be used.

(9) Please indicate that the manuscript is collected by the Book and Newspaper Introduction Editorial Department.

(10) All manuscripts, whether published or not, will not be returned. If you need to return them, you should declare it in advance and attach sufficient postage stamps.

(11) Remuneration for texts is divided into three types: three yuan, two yuan, and one yuan per thousand words. The same applies to each picture and photo. If there are special manuscripts, the remuneration will be calculated separately.

Youth Space

Northern Journey Impressions 215

— Su Ling

(10) News of Spring

"...Friends, has the solid ice of the northern frontier melted? Are snowflakes still flying in the sky?... Ah, spring has arrived in Jiangnan, the shallow grasses are green, the peach petals are unfolding... Friends, my wandering friends, I now send a small sprig of peach blossoms and a small branch of willow from Jiangnan to the distant northern frontier, so that you may receive news of spring from your homeland in this land of snow and ice..."

Ah, how greatly I thank you for sending me news of spring, my dear friend!

Outside the window, the jagged, withered branches still bear snow, snowflakes are fluttering down again, and the ice on the river is still frozen solid and unbroken... Haha, this is precisely the season of new spring in Jiangnan! I pondered, I thought of the coming of spring in Jiangnan, that serene, winding little river, lying amidst tender reds and fresh greens, the south wind gently caressing the willow branches on the bank, dotting the still surface of the water, the fallen petals of the Yao flowers sometimes falling languidly, whereupon the fish are startled, rising to the surface, thinking they have found food, chasing after it, finally discouraged and retreating back into the deep water, flipping their tails, the still water splashing with light waves, rippling into wandering whirlpools, the sun peeking from behind the green leaves, smiling.

Whenever I hear the delicate and simple cries of the flower-selling girls in the streets and alleys, I know that spring has arrived, and I always go to take a look at that little river.

But now, I am wandering in the northern frontier, and a friend from Jiangnan is painstakingly telling me the news of spring. However, alas, the snowy fields of the northern frontier are still stirring with cold winds, the delicate necks of the girls are still wrapped in fur collars, and where can I go to see that little river?

"The Songhua River will not thaw until June. When the ice on the Songhua River thaws, new green will be seen on the tree branches, the grasslands will gradually turn green, and coats can be taken off our bodies—by then, I'm afraid spring in Jiangnan will have faded."

"Oh," I dazedly gazed at the gray sky, the snow-covered withered branches, and the gentle dance of snowflakes, "by then, by then spring in Jiangnan will have returned, the peach blossoms will have withered, the willows will have aged, and the water in the little river will have changed color. By then, the girls in the city will have changed into light, thin gauze dresses—but here, we are just beginning to see green leaves emerging from the melting snow, breathing the breath of spring."

—This is the miracle of nature.

So, I tucked the flattened peach petals and willow branches into the pages of my book and continued reading the letter from my Jiangnan friend.

"...Ah, friend, this will evoke your memories of spring... Surely you will not forget the cherry blossoms of Xuanwu Lake, the peach blossoms of Longhua, and the willows of West Lake. Even that still little river that we happened upon during one of our walks will likely enter your memory..."

Jiaotong University Promotes Swimming Program 216

— Quan

Jiaotong University has a swimming pool that other universities (the eight universities that joined the Jiangnan Sports Association) do not have. Their swimming results should dominate Jiangnan and be the best. However, in this swimming championship competition, they were greatly defeated by Jinan, with a score of seventeen to forty-six. What is the reason for this? It is a matter of whether or not they have made the effort to promote swimming. Although Jinan does not have the facilities of a swimming pool, they have made great efforts to promote swimming. Before the summer vacation, the team members camped out at Qingyang Port to practice swimming, and after the summer vacation, they practiced all day at the YMCA swimming pool. The adequacy of their preparation is self-evident. Although Jiaotong University has a swimming pool, it is only open for a short period of time, starting every year from April or May and closing at the end of September. Also, there are specific hours during which the pool is open. During the summer vacation, some team members also return home. Therefore, although there is a swimming pool, it is abandoned and not used. Practice only started two weeks before the competition, so how could they have achieved amazing results? The sports authorities, in view of this, have formulated a swimming promotion program in order to avenge this year's loss when competing with other universities next year. The program includes: (1) The swimming pool will continue to be open this winter. Heating pipes will be installed at the bottom of the pool to increase the water temperature, or a stove will be installed to prevent team members from catching a cold during practice. (2) Once the team members are selected, the gymnasium must set aside time for them to practice. During the designated time, non-team members are not allowed to mingle, and team members are not allowed to avoid practice without reason. With diligent practice, progress will be easy. (3) Swimming experts will be hired to provide guidance. Negotiations have been completed. Mr. Chen Yuehe, a overseas Chinese from Nanyang, will be the swimming instructor, and Mr. Shen Guoquan, the director of physical education at the school, is also an expert. With guidance, the results should be excellent. (4) The team members' physical condition will be checked by the school doctor at any time. Any nutritional deficiencies will be notified and attention paid to them. (5) Next year, they will join various ocean swimming competition groups to learn from each other. They also plan to invite various swimming groups to participate in friendly competitions this year. All of the above programs have been submitted by the director of physical education, Shen Guoquan, to the chairman of the sports committee, Zhong Weicheng, who will then submit them to the president for approval and implementation. Various expenses have also been allocated. The school does have a lot of swimming talent. For example, in the short distance swimming competition, the Jiaotong University team member competed with a Mr. Dong of the Jinan team, only losing by one meter to take second place. In long distance swimming, Huang Taiji, Ye Wu, Xu Yaotang, and others are all talented. If they can be given good guidance and long-term practice, Jinan may not be their opponent. I sincerely hope that the team can make good use of their skills and live up to the excellent facilities.

Revival of the Wall Newspaper Craze 217

— Ding

|Correspondence|

Jia,

I have received the letter you sent me the day before yesterday. I wanted to reply to you right away, but I am really busy with my studies this year. I lock myself in the library every day, and recently I have been preparing for the monthly exams, so I haven't even had time to write you a letter. I suppose you must be as anxious as the last time, like an ant on a hot pot, pacing back and forth in the gatehouse all day long, right?

Some of the male students in our school pooled their money to create a wall newspaper, posting everything about our female students' actions, forcing me to be as wary as if I were guarding against thieves, being careful in every way. But if I'm not careful, they find out anyway, which is really hateful.

It's been more than three weeks since the start of this semester, and there hasn't been a single wall newspaper. I was really happy! This morning, after finishing my first class, I walked past Zibin Hall on my way back to the dormitory, and I saw that "Short Wave Radio," which is known for its quick news and well-organized structure, was published again. "Splendor," sponsored by the preparatory department's association, still put on a face of impartiality and fairness and met with us. At the same time, there was also a "Sacrificial Sound," which was newly published, but I don't know who sponsored it. The content is really interesting. A Fang, who specializes in being a palace detective, also wrote a piece called "Eastern Palace Chronicles" and posted it there. Although this opening piece doesn't write about any facts, it has a very laughable vow. I copied it down:

South dormitory in front,

Zibin Hall behind,

If A Fang writes about the Eastern Palace again,

He'll turn into a monkey and be locked on the fourth floor.

Jia, I really wish he would immediately turn into a monkey and be locked on the fourth floor, so that he wouldn't write about our affairs and let everyone know. There's another piece called "Father and Son," which is a strange piece of writing. I read it for a long time and didn't know who he was talking about. I guess there's probably no such fact, and that "Jade Without Flaws" is just gossiping. Now I'm copying it down for you to see, do you think there is such a sinister person in the world?

"This is a fact, a truly meaningful fact. We don't think that if a father and son have different ideas, the son is unfilial. If the son's ideas are clearer than his father's, the so-called ideas of the latecomers, and the old father wants to scold his son for being unfilial, we will help the young man clear his name.

But if the son's ideas go astray, as if he has been tempted by the Communist Party and wants to fight with his father, this is the son's fundamental mistake. If a good young man is tempted, then we must attack the son for being improper.

A middle school student in our school, praising him in Director Chen's tone, 'This is a very capable young man.' In Director Chen's eyes, the so-called capable young man is nothing more than being able to run errands for him. I am very sure that before he was bewitched by the troublemakers, he was indeed a clear-headed person. He can write articles, take photos, and be able to handle matters for everyone. Honestly, when the Communist Party sees such a talent, they will definitely try to take him as a disciple. So they came up with a way to first give him sweet bait, hook the fat fish, easily get him, and then he escaped back.

This classmate... his father is a brigade commander in the National Army, with seven or eight concubines. According to Xiong, these many concubines are all trophies from winning battles. He is the only son, and he spends a lot of money at school. When the Zhongshan Western Restaurant opened, he treated guests for seven or eight yuan at a time. Most of the people he invites are female classmates, and this semester he has introduced seven or eight female classmates to Fudan.

He used to be the chairman of the student union, and it is said that Chen used his influence to get him elected. He has handled major events, and of course he spends a lot of money to seek pleasure with his girlfriends, and has never thought of red revolution. Once the good meat is in hand, how can they give it up? So the prole comrades came up with a sinister plan. The first step was to have him write a letter to his father, saying, 'Since our father and son have different opinions, it would be better to break off relations.' When the brigade commander father saw that his young brigade commander was being seduced, and his only heir, he was unwilling to let him run wild, so he sent his son a top-priority telegram, scolding him fiercely, and even appended the shocking sentence, 'Otherwise, I will stop sending money.' Indeed, this comrade is too stupid, and he didn't think of other ways. Perhaps I forgot that the prole comrades promised to give him other money. But the show has only reached this step, and the matter is not over. We have to see how capable prole Comrade × is, and whether he can defeat the brigade commander.

This is a fact. The second half of the facts, I will ask about it and then tell you. But if Comrade × goes into hiding, then the reporter can't talk about it anymore."

Jia, how do you feel after reading this? If this is a fact,

You want me to tell you about my life, but I'm telling you so much about wall newspapers. Are you happy to read it? In reality, I'm living a monotonous school life, and there's nothing to tell you. I only hope that you send me letters every day to liven up my life.

But I still have to tell you something strange, which is that the middle school principal saw that piece "Father and Son" and asked the secretary-general to investigate the wall newspaper, at least to have them correct it. It has now been turned over to the training office.

I don't have time during the day, and I'm afraid of being caught by my classmates and making a fuss, so I waited until they were in bed, lit a candle, and secretly wrote this letter to you. I originally had a lot more to say to you, but my sister is already awake, and I'm afraid she'll make so much noise that the whole room of classmates will know, so I'll have to stop writing. Fortunately, Saturday is coming again, and I'll still be waiting for you in the same park to go to the movies together.

I'm sending you a sweet kiss to say goodbye,

Ding, in Jiangwan.

Youth Garden Manuscript Guidelines 218

(1) The text should focus on discussions of youth issues, news and essays about domestic and foreign schools or students, descriptions of school life, and essays. The style is not limited.

(2) Books are limited to those concerning youth issues.

(3) Photos of youth life (such as sports, travel, visits, dramas, lectures, gatherings, exhibitions, various competitions, etc.), school news, and youth movements are all welcome, whether individual or group.

(4) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

Peace! 219

After Zhang Xueliang returned to Shenyang from Beidaihe, he convened a meeting of prominent figures from various provinces and regions in the Northeast and decided to issue a telegram advocating peace on September 18. Subsequently, the First Army, led by Yu Xuezhong, and the Second Army, led by Wang Shuchang, entered the customs. Their vanguard arrived in Tianjin on the 21st and entered Beiping on the 25th. The Jin army had withdrawn in advance, and the situation took on a new look.
